>> Issue: [B824:url_found] url_found
   Severity: Medium   Confidence: Medium
   Location: /home/blue/PyPIAgent/Dataset/study/unzip_benign/acryl_datahub-1.0.0.3rc2/acryl_datahub-1.0.0.3rc2/src/datahub/ingestion/source/redshift/query.py:683
   More Info: https://bandit.readthedocs.io/en/latest/plugins/b824_url_found.html
682	
683	        return rf"""-- DataHub Redshift Source temp table DDL query
684	select
685	    *
686	from (
687	    select
688	        session_id,
689	        transaction_id,
690	        start_time,
691	        userid,
692	        REGEXP_REPLACE(REGEXP_SUBSTR(REGEXP_REPLACE(query_text,'\\\\n','\\n'), '(CREATE(?:[\\n\\s\\t]+(?:temp|temporary))?(?:[\\n\\s\\t]+)table(?:[\\n\\s\\t]+)[^\\n\\s\\t()-]+)', 0, 1, 'ipe'),'[\\n\\s\\t]+',' ',1,'p') as create_command,
693	        query_text,
694	        row_number() over (
695	            partition by session_id, TRIM(query_text)
696	            order by start_time desc
697	        ) rn
698	    from (
699	        select
700	            pid as session_id,
701	            xid as transaction_id,
702	            starttime as start_time,
703	            type,
704	            query_text,
705	            userid
706	        from (
707	            select
708	                starttime,
709	                pid,
710	                xid,
711	                type,
712	                userid,
713	                LISTAGG(case
714	                    when LEN(RTRIM(text)) = 0 then text
715	                    else RTRIM(text)
716	                end,
717	                '') within group (
718	                    order by sequence
719	                ) as query_text
720	            from
721	                SVL_STATEMENTTEXT
722	            where
723	                type in ('DDL', 'QUERY')
